ARQUIVO: README.md
========================================================================================================================

This is a [Next.js](https://nextjs.org) project bootstrapped with [`create-next-app`](https://nextjs.org/docs/app/api-reference/cli/create-next-app).

## Getting Started

First, run the development server:

```bash
npm run dev
# or
yarn dev
# or
pnpm dev
# or
bun dev
```

Open [http://localhost:3000](http://localhost:3000) with your browser to see the result.

You can start editing the page by modifying `app/page.tsx`. The page auto-updates as you edit the file.

This project uses [`next/font`](https://nextjs.org/docs/app/building-your-application/optimizing/fonts) to automatically optimize and load [Geist](https://vercel.com/font), a new font family for Vercel.

## Learn More

To learn more about Next.js, take a look at the following resources:

- [Next.js Documentation](https://nextjs.org/docs) - learn about Next.js features and API.
- [Learn Next.js](https://nextjs.org/learn) - an interactive Next.js tutorial.

You can check out [the Next.js GitHub repository](https://github.com/vercel/next.js) - your feedback and contributions are welcome!

## Deploy on Vercel

The easiest way to deploy your Next.js app is to use the [Vercel Platform](https://vercel.com/new?utm_medium=default-template&filter=next.js&utm_source=create-next-app&utm_campaign=create-next-app-readme) from the creators of Next.js.

Check out our [Next.js deployment documentation](https://nextjs.org/docs/app/building-your-application/deploying) for more details.

========================================================================================================================
ARQUIVO: src\app\(auth)\login\page.tsx
========================================================================================================================

'use client';

import { useEffect, useState } from 'react';
import { useRouter } from 'next/navigation';
import { useAuth } from '@/hooks/use-auth';
import { login as loginService } from '@/services/auth.service';

export default function LoginPage() {
  const router = useRouter();
  const {
    token,
    user,
    isAuthenticated,
    loading,
    setSession,
    hydrateSession,
  } = useAuth();

  const [email, setEmail] = useState('');
  const [password, setPassword] = useState('');
  const [submitting, setSubmitting] = useState(false);
  const [error, setError] = useState<string | null>(null);

  useEffect(() => {
    hydrateSession();
  }, [hydrateSession]);

  useEffect(() => {
    if (loading) return;
    if (!token || !user || !isAuthenticated) return;

    if (user.role === 'OPERADOR') {
      router.replace('/operacao');
      return;
    }

    if (user.role === 'ADMIN' || user.role === 'MASTER') {
      router.replace('/admin');
      return;
    }

    router.replace('/');
  }, [loading, token, user, isAuthenticated, router]);

  const handleSubmit = async (event: React.FormEvent<HTMLFormElement>) => {
    event.preventDefault();
    setError(null);
    setSubmitting(true);

    try {
      const response = await loginService(email, password);

      if (!response?.token || !response?.user) {
        throw new Error('Resposta invÃ¡lida da autenticaÃ§Ã£o.');
      }

      setSession(response.token, response.user);

      if (response.user.role === 'OPERADOR') {
        router.replace('/operacao');
        return;
      }

      if (response.user.role === 'ADMIN' || response.user.role === 'MASTER') {
        router.replace('/admin');
        return;
      }

      router.replace('/');
    } catch (err) {
      const message = err instanceof Error ? err.message : 'E-mail ou senha invÃ¡lidos.';
      setError(message);
    } finally {
      setSubmitting(false);
    }
  };

  if (loading) {
    return (
      <div className="flex min-h-screen items-center justify-center bg-zinc-950 text-white">
        Carregando...
      </div>
    );
  }

  return (
    <div className="flex min-h-screen items-center justify-center bg-zinc-950 px-4">
      <div className="w-full max-w-md rounded-2xl border border-zinc-800 bg-zinc-900 p-8 shadow-lg">
        <h1 className="mb-6 text-2xl font-bold text-white">Entrar</h1>

        <form onSubmit={handleSubmit} className="space-y-4">
          <div>
            <label className="mb-1 block text-sm text-zinc-300">E-mail</label>
            <input
              type="email"
              className="w-full rounded-lg border border-zinc-700 bg-zinc-950 px-4 py-3 text-white outline-none"
              value={email}
              onChange={(e) => setEmail(e.target.value)}
              required
              autoComplete="email"
            />
          </div>

          <div>
            <label className="mb-1 block text-sm text-zinc-300">Senha</label>
            <input
              type="password"
              className="w-full rounded-lg border border-zinc-700 bg-zinc-950 px-4 py-3 text-white outline-none"
              value={password}
              onChange={(e) => setPassword(e.target.value)}
              required
              autoComplete="current-password"
            />
          </div>

          {error && (
            <div className="rounded-lg border border-red-500/30 bg-red-500/10 px-4 py-3 text-sm text-red-200">
              {error}
            </div>
          )}

          <button
            type="submit"
            disabled={submitting}
            className="w-full rounded-lg bg-white px-4 py-3 font-medium text-black transition hover:bg-zinc-200 disabled:cursor-not-allowed disabled:opacity-60"
          >
            {submitting ? 'Entrando...' : 'Entrar'}
          </button>
        </form>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

========================================================================================================================
ARQUIVO: src\app\admin\encomendas\page.tsx
========================================================================================================================

'use client';

import { useEffect, useMemo, useState } from 'react';
import { useRouter } from 'next/navigation';
import {
  Search,
  RefreshCw,
  Plus,
  Eye,
  Pencil,
  Package,
  Truck,
  ClipboardList,
  CheckCircle2,
  Clock3,
  CircleAlert,
  Filter,
  MoreHorizontal,
} from 'lucide-react';
import { useAuth } from '@/hooks/use-auth';
import { useDeliveries } from '@/hooks/use-deliveries';
import { CrudModal } from '@/components/admin/CrudModal';
import { Button } from '@/components/ui/button';
import { Card, CardContent, CardHeader, CardTitle } from '@/components/ui/card';
import { Input } from '@/components/ui/input';
import { Badge } from '@/components/ui/badge';

type DeliveryFormData = {
  recipient: string;
  sender: string;
  trackingCode: string;
  carrier: string;
  status: string;
  note: string;
  unit: string;
  block: string;
};

type DeliveryRow = {
  id: string;
  recipient: string;
  sender?: string;
  trackingCode?: string;
  carrier?: string;
  status?: string;
  note?: string;
  unit?: string;
  block?: string;
  createdAt?: string;
};

type Filters = {
  search: string;
  status: string;
};

const API_BASE =
  process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_API_URL?.replace(/\/$/, '') ?? 'https://sapinhoprod.v8seguranca.com.br/api/v1';

function normalizeDeliveries(data: unknown): DeliveryRow[] {
  if (Array.isArray(data)) return data as DeliveryRow[];
  if (data && typeof data === 'object' && Array.isArray((data as { data?: unknown[] }).data)) {
    return (data as { data: DeliveryRow[] }).data;
  }
  return [];
}

function safeText(value: unknown, fallback = '') {
  if (value === null || value === undefined) return fallback;
  const text = String(value).trim();
  return text.length ? text : fallback;
}

function normalizeStatus(value: unknown) {
  return safeText(value, 'pendente').toLowerCase();
}

function matchesSearch(row: DeliveryRow, term: string) {
  if (!term) return true;
  const q = term.toLowerCase();
  return [
    row.recipient,
    row.sender,
    row.trackingCode,
    row.carrier,
    row.status,
    row.note,
    row.unit,
    row.block,
  ]
    .filter(Boolean)
    .some((value) => String(value).toLowerCase().includes(q));
}

function StatCard({
  title,
  value,
  icon: Icon,
  hint,
}: {
  title: string;
  value: string;
  icon: React.ComponentType<{ className?: string }>;
  hint: string;
}) {
  return (
    <Card className="border-white/10 bg-white/5 text-white">
      <CardHeader className="flex flex-row items-start justify-between space-y-0 pb-2">
        <CardTitle className="text-sm font-medium text-slate-300">{title}</CardTitle>
        <Icon className="h-4 w-4 text-slate-400" />
      </CardHeader>
      <CardContent>
        <div className="text-2xl font-semibold">{value}</div>
        <p className="mt-1 text-xs text-slate-400">{hint}</p>
      </CardContent>
    </Card>
  );
}

function DeliveryForm({
  initialData,
  onSubmit,
  onCancel,
  loading = false,
}: {
  initialData?: Partial<DeliveryFormData>;
  onSubmit: (data: DeliveryFormData) => Promise<void> | void;
  onCancel: () => void;
  loading?: boolean;
}) {
  const [form, setForm] = useState<DeliveryFormData>({
    recipient: '',
    sender: '',
    trackingCode: '',
    carrier: '',
    status: 'pendente',
    note: '',
    unit: '',
    block: '',
    ...initialData,
  });

  useEffect(() => {
    setForm({
      recipient: '',
      sender: '',
      trackingCode: '',
      carrier: '',
      status: 'pendente',
      note: '',
      unit: '',
      block: '',
      ...initialData,
    });
  }, [initialData]);

  const handleSubmit = async (event: React.FormEvent) => {
    event.preventDefault();
    await onSubmit(form);
  };

  const setField = (field: keyof DeliveryFormData, value: string) => {
    setForm((prev) => ({ ...prev, [field]: value }));
  };

  return (
    <form onSubmit={handleSubmit} className="space-y-5">
      <div className="grid gap-5 md:grid-cols-2">
        <label className="space-y-2">
          <span className="text-sm text-slate-300">DestinatÃ¡rio</span>
          <input
            type="text"
            value={form.recipient}
            onChange={(e) => setField('recipient', e.target.value)}
            className="w-full rounded-2xl border border-white/10 bg-slate-900 px-4 py-3 text-white outline-none placeholder:text-slate-500"
            placeholder="Nome do destinatÃ¡rio"
            required
          />
        </label>

        <label className="space-y-2">
          <span className="text-sm text-slate-300">Remetente</span>
          <input
            type="text"
            value={form.sender}
            onChange={(e) => setField('sender', e.target.value)}
            className="w-full rounded-2xl border border-white/10 bg-slate-900 px-4 py-3 text-white outline-none placeholder:text-slate-500"
            placeholder="Nome do remetente"
          />
        </label>

        <label className="space-y-2">
          <span className="text-sm text-slate-300">CÃ³digo de rastreio</span>
          <input
            type="text"
            value={form.trackingCode}
            onChange={(e) => setField('trackingCode', e.target.value)}
            className="w-full rounded-2xl border border-white/10 bg-slate-900 px-4 py-3 text-white outline-none placeholder:text-slate-500"
            placeholder="Ex.: BR123456789"
          />
        </label>

        <label className="space-y-2">
          <span className="text-sm text-slate-300">Transportadora</span>
          <input
            type="text"
            value={form.carrier}
            onChange={(e) => setField('carrier', e.target.value)}
            className="w-full rounded-2xl border border-white/10 bg-slate-900 px-4 py-3 text-white outline-none placeholder:text-slate-500"
            placeholder="Nome da transportadora"
          />
        </label>

        <label className="space-y-2">
          <span className="text-sm text-slate-300">Bloco</span>
          <input
            type="text"
            value={form.block}
            onChange={(e) => setField('block', e.target.value)}
            className="w-full rounded-2xl border border-white/10 bg-slate-900 px-4 py-3 text-white outline-none placeholder:text-slate-500"
            placeholder="Ex.: A"
          />
        </label>

        <label className="space-y-2">
          <span className="text-sm text-slate-300">Unidade</span>
          <input
            type="text"
            value={form.unit}
            onChange={(e) => setField('unit', e.target.value)}
            className="w-full rounded-2xl border border-white/10 bg-slate-900 px-4 py-3 text-white outline-none placeholder:text-slate-500"
            placeholder="Ex.: 101"
          />
        </label>

        <label className="space-y-2 md:col-span-2">
          <span className="text-sm text-slate-300">Status</span>
          <select
            value={form.status}
            onChange={(e) => setField('status', e.target.value)}
            className="w-full rounded-2xl border border-white/10 bg-slate-900 px-4 py-3 text-white outline-none"
          >
            <option value="pendente">Pendente</option>
            <option value="recebido">Recebido</option>
            <option value="entregue">Entregue</option>
            <option value="retido">Retido</option>
            <option value="devolvido">Devolvido</option>
          </select>
        </label>

        <label className="space-y-2 md:col-span-2">
          <span className="text-sm text-slate-300">ObservaÃ§Ã£o</span>
          <textarea
            value={form.note}
            onChange={(e) => setField('note', e.target.value)}
            rows={5}
            className="w-full rounded-2xl border border-white/10 bg-slate-900 px-4 py-3 text-white outline-none placeholder:text-slate-500"
            placeholder="InformaÃ§Ãµes adicionais..."
          />
        </label>
      </div>

      <div className="flex flex-wrap justify-end gap-3 pt-2">
        <button
          type="button"
          onClick={onCancel}
          className="rounded-xl border border-white/10 bg-white/10 px-4 py-3 text-sm text-white transition hover:bg-white/15"
        >
          Cancelar
        </button>

        <button
          type="submit"
          disabled={loading}
          className="rounded-xl bg-white px-4 py-3 text-sm font-medium text-slate-950 transition hover:bg-slate-200 disabled:cursor-not-allowed disabled:opacity-60"
        >
          {loading ? 'Salvando...' : 'Salvar na API'}
        </button>
      </div>
    </form>
  );
}

export default function EncomendasPage() {
  const router = useRouter();
  const { user, loading: authLoading, isAuthenticated } = useAuth();
  const {
    data: deliveriesData,
    isLoading: deliveriesLoading,
    error: deliveriesError,
    refetch: refetchDeliveries,
  } = useDeliveries({ limit: 200 });

  const [mounted, setMounted] = useState(false);
  const [filters, setFilters] = useState<Filters>({
    search: '',
    status: 'all',
  });
  const [openCreate, setOpenCreate] = useState(false);
  const [openEdit, setOpenEdit] = useState(false);
  const [selected, setSelected] = useState<DeliveryRow | null>(null);
  const [saving, setSaving] = useState(false);
  const [deletingId, setDeletingId] = useState<string | null>(null);

  useEffect(() => {
    setMounted(true);
  }, []);

  useEffect(() => {
    if (!mounted || authLoading) return;

    if (!isAuthenticated || !user) {
      router.replace('/login');
      return;
    }

    if (!['ADMIN', 'MASTER'].includes(String(user.role))) {
      router.replace('/admin');
    }
  }, [mounted, authLoading, isAuthenticated, user, router]);

  const deliveries = useMemo(() => normalizeDeliveries(deliveriesData), [deliveriesData]);

  const filteredDeliveries = useMemo(() => {
    return deliveries.filter((row) => {
      const statusOk = filters.status === 'all' || normalizeStatus(row.status) === filters.status;
      const searchOk = matchesSearch(row, filters.search);
      return statusOk && searchOk;
    });
  }, [deliveries, filters]);

  const stats = useMemo(() => {
    const total = deliveries.length;
    const pendentes = deliveries.filter((d) => normalizeStatus(d.status) === 'pendente').length;
    const recebidas = deliveries.filter((d) => normalizeStatus(d.status) === 'recebido').length;
    const entregues = deliveries.filter((d) => normalizeStatus(d.status) === 'entregue').length;

    return { total, pendentes, recebidas, entregues };
  }, [deliveries]);

  const handleRefresh = async () => {
    await refetchDeliveries();
  };

  const openNew = () => {
    setSelected(null);
    setOpenCreate(true);
  };

  const openEditDelivery = (row: DeliveryRow) => {
    setSelected(row);
    setOpenEdit(true);
  };

  const closeModals = () => {
    setOpenCreate(false);
    setOpenEdit(false);
    setSelected(null);
  };

  async function createDelivery(data: DeliveryFormData) {
    setSaving(true);
    try {
      const response = await fetch(`${API_BASE}/deliveries`, {
        method: 'POST',
        headers: {
          'Content-Type': 'application/json',
          Authorization: `Bearer ${localStorage.getItem('accessToken') ?? ''}`,
        },
        body: JSON.stringify({
          recipient: data.recipient,
          sender: data.sender,
          trackingCode: data.trackingCode,
          carrier: data.carrier,
          status: data.status,
          note: data.note,
          unit: data.unit,
          block: data.block,
        }),
      });

      if (!response.ok) {
        const message = await response.text();
        throw new Error(message || 'Erro ao criar encomenda');
      }

      setOpenCreate(false);
      await handleRefresh();
    } finally {
      setSaving(false);
    }
  }

  async function updateDelivery(data: DeliveryFormData) {
    if (!selected?.id) return;

    setSaving(true);
    try {
      const response = await fetch(`${API_BASE}/deliveries/${selected.id}`, {
        method: 'PUT',
        headers: {
          'Content-Type': 'application/json',
          Authorization: `Bearer ${localStorage.getItem('accessToken') ?? ''}`,
        },
        body: JSON.stringify({
          recipient: data.recipient,
          sender: data.sender,
          trackingCode: data.trackingCode,
          carrier: data.carrier,
          status: data.status,
          note: data.note,
          unit: data.unit,
          block: data.block,
        }),
      });

      if (!response.ok) {
        const message = await response.text();
        throw new Error(message || 'Erro ao atualizar encomenda');
      }

      setOpenEdit(false);
      setSelected(null);
      await handleRefresh();
    } finally {
      setSaving(false);
    }
  }

  async function deleteDelivery(id: string) {
    const confirmed = window.confirm('Deseja excluir esta encomenda?');
    if (!confirmed) return;

    setDeletingId(id);
    try {
      const response = await fetch(`${API_BASE}/deliveries/${id}`, {
        method: 'DELETE',
        headers: {
          Authorization: `Bearer ${localStorage.getItem('accessToken') ?? ''}`,
        },
      });

      if (!response.ok) {
        const message = await response.text();
        throw new Error(message || 'Erro ao excluir encomenda');
      }

      await handleRefresh();
    } finally {
      setDeletingId(null);
    }
  }

  if (!mounted || authLoading) {
    return (
      <div className="flex min-h-[60vh] items-center justify-center rounded-3xl border border-white/10 bg-white/5 text-white">
        Carregando painel...
      </div>
    );
  }

  if (!isAuthenticated || !user) return null;

  return (
    <div className="space-y-6 text-white">
      <section className="rounded-3xl border border-white/10 bg-white/5 p-5 backdrop-blur">
        <div className="flex flex-col gap-4 lg:flex-row lg:items-end lg:justify-between">
          <div>
            <p className="text-xs uppercase tracking-[0.22em] text-slate-400">AdministraÃ§Ã£o</p>
            <h1 className="mt-2 text-2xl font-semibold">Encomendas</h1>
            <p className="mt-2 max-w-2xl text-sm text-slate-400">
              Controle de entregas, recebimentos e status com integraÃ§Ã£o direta Ã  API real.
            </p>
          </div>

          <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-3">
            <Button
              onClick={openNew}
              className="inline-flex items-center gap-2 rounded-xl bg-white px-4 py-3 text-slate-950 hover:bg-slate-200"
            >
              <Plus className="h-4 w-4" />
              Novo
            </Button>

            <Button
              variant="outline"
              onClick={handleRefresh}
              className="inline-flex items-center gap-2 border-white/10 bg-white/5 text-white hover:bg-white/10"
            >
              <RefreshCw className="h-4 w-4" />
              Atualizar
            </Button>
          </div>
        </div>
      </section>

      <section className="grid gap-4 md:grid-cols-2 xl:grid-cols-4">
        <StatCard title="Total" value={deliveriesLoading ? '...' : String(stats.total)} icon={Package} hint="Todas as encomendas" />
        <StatCard title="Pendentes" value={deliveriesLoading ? '...' : String(stats.pendentes)} icon={Clock3} hint="Aguardando aÃ§Ã£o" />
        <StatCard title="Recebidas" value={deliveriesLoading ? '...' : String(stats.recebidas)} icon={ClipboardList} hint="Registradas na portaria" />
        <StatCard title="Entregues" value={deliveriesLoading ? '...' : String(stats.entregues)} icon={CheckCircle2} hint="JÃ¡ liberadas ao morador" />
      </section>

      <section className="rounded-3xl border border-white/10 bg-white/5 p-5 backdrop-blur">
        <div className="grid gap-3 lg:grid-cols-[1.5fr_0.8fr]">
          <label className="flex items-center gap-3 rounded-2xl border border-white/10 bg-slate-950/60 px-4 py-3">
            <Search className="h-4 w-4 text-slate-400" />
            <Input
              value={filters.search}
              onChange={(e) => setFilters((prev) => ({ ...prev, search: e.target.value }))}
              placeholder="Buscar por destinatÃ¡rio, rastreio, transportadora..."
              className="border-0 bg-transparent p-0 text-white shadow-none placeholder:text-slate-500 focus-visible:ring-0"
            />
          </label>

          <label className="rounded-2xl border border-white/10 bg-slate-950/60 px-4 py-3">
            <select
              value={filters.status}
              onChange={(e) => setFilters((prev) => ({ ...prev, status: e.target.value }))}
              className="w-full bg-transparent text-sm outline-none"
            >
              <option value="all">Todos os status</option>
              <option value="pendente">Pendente</option>
              <option value="recebido">Recebido</option>
              <option value="entregue">Entregue</option>
              <option value="retido">Retido</option>
              <option value="devolvido">Devolvido</option>
            </select>
          </label>
        </div>
      </section>

      {deliveriesError ? (
        <div className="rounded-3xl border border-red-500/30 bg-red-500/10 p-5 text-sm text-red-100">
          NÃ£o foi possÃ­vel carregar as encomendas.
        </div>
      ) : null}

      <section className="overflow-hidden rounded-3xl border border-white/10 bg-white/5 backdrop-blur">
        <div className="flex items-center justify-between border-b border-white/10 px-5 py-4">
          <div>
            <h2 className="text-lg font-semibold">Lista de encomendas</h2>
            <p className="text-sm text-slate-400">
              {filteredDeliveries.length} registro(s) encontrado(s)
            </p>
          </div>
          <Filter className="h-5 w-5 text-slate-400" />
        </div>

        {filteredDeliveries.length === 0 ? (
          <div className="px-5 py-10">
            <div className="rounded-2xl border border-dashed border-white/10 bg-slate-950/50 p-8 text-center">
              <CircleAlert className="mx-auto h-10 w-10 text-slate-400" />
              <h3 className="mt-3 text-base font-medium">Nenhuma encomenda encontrada</h3>
              <p className="mt-1 text-sm text-slate-400">
                Ajuste os filtros ou clique em Novo para cadastrar.
              </p>
            </div>
          </div>
        ) : (
          <div className="divide-y divide-white/10">
            {filteredDeliveries.map((delivery) => (
              <div
                key={delivery.id}
                className="grid gap-4 px-5 py-4 lg:grid-cols-[1.4fr_0.8fr_0.7fr_0.8fr_auto] lg:items-center"
              >
                <div>
                  <p className="font-medium text-white">{safeText(delivery.recipient, 'Sem destinatÃ¡rio')}</p>
                  <p className="text-sm text-slate-400">
                    {safeText(delivery.block, 'â€”')} / {safeText(delivery.unit, 'â€”')}
                  </p>
                </div>

                <div className="text-sm text-slate-300">
                  {safeText(delivery.trackingCode, 'Sem rastreio')}
                </div>

                <div className="text-sm text-slate-300">
                  {safeText(delivery.carrier, 'Sem transportadora')}
                </div>

                <div>
                  <Badge
                    className={
                      normalizeStatus(delivery.status) === 'entregue'
                        ? 'bg-emerald-500/15 text-emerald-300 hover:bg-emerald-500/20'
                        : normalizeStatus(delivery.status) === 'recebido'
                          ? 'bg-sky-500/15 text-sky-300 hover:bg-sky-500/20'
                          : normalizeStatus(delivery.status) === 'retido'
                            ? 'bg-red-500/15 text-red-300 hover:bg-red-500/20'
                            : 'bg-amber-500/15 text-amber-300 hover:bg-amber-500/20'
                    }
                  >
                    {safeText(delivery.status, 'pendente')}
                  </Badge>
                </div>

                <div className="flex items-center justify-end gap-2">
                  <Button
                    size="icon"
                    variant="outline"
                    className="border-white/10 bg-white/5 text-white hover:bg-white/10"
                    aria-label="Visualizar encomenda"
                  >
                    <Eye className="h-4 w-4" />
                  </Button>

                  <Button
                    size="icon"
                    variant="outline"
                    onClick={() => openEditDelivery(delivery)}
                    className="border-white/10 bg-white/5 text-white hover:bg-white/10"
                    aria-label="Editar encomenda"
                  >
                    <Pencil className="h-4 w-4" />
                  </Button>

                  <Button
                    size="icon"
                    variant="outline"
                    onClick={() => deleteDelivery(delivery.id)}
                    disabled={deletingId === delivery.id}
                    className="border-white/10 bg-white/5 text-white hover:bg-white/10"
                    aria-label="Excluir encomenda"
                  >
                    <MoreHorizontal className="h-4 w-4" />
                  </Button>
                </div>
              </div>
            ))}
          </div>
        )}
      </section>

      <CrudModal
        open={openCreate}
        title="Nova encomenda"
        description="Cadastre uma nova encomenda na API externa."
        onClose={closeModals}
        maxWidth="xl"
      >
        <DeliveryForm onSubmit={createDelivery} onCancel={closeModals} loading={saving} />
      </CrudModal>

      <CrudModal
        open={openEdit}
        title="Editar encomenda"
        description="Atualize os dados da encomenda selecionada."
        onClose={closeModals}
        maxWidth="xl"
      >
        <DeliveryForm
          initialData={
            selected
              ? {
                  recipient: selected.recipient,
                  sender: selected.sender ?? '',
                  trackingCode: selected.trackingCode ?? '',
                  carrier: selected.carrier ?? '',
                  status: normalizeStatus(selected.status),
                  note: selected.note ?? '',
                  unit: selected.unit ?? '',
                  block: selected.block ?? '',
                }
              : undefined
          }
          onSubmit={updateDelivery}
          onCancel={closeModals}
          loading={saving}
        />
      </CrudModal>
    </div>
  );
}

'use client';

import { useEffect, useState } from 'react';
import { useRouter } from 'next/navigation';
import { useAuth } from '@/hooks/use-auth';
import { Sidebar } from '@/components/layout/sidebar';
import { Header } from '@/components/layout/header';

export default function AdminLayout({
  children,
}: {
  children: React.ReactNode;
}) {
  const router = useRouter();
  const { user, loading: authLoading, isAuthenticated } = useAuth();
  const [mounted, setMounted] = useState(false);
  const [sidebarCollapsed, setSidebarCollapsed] = useState(false);

  const allowedRoles = ['ADMIN', 'MASTER'];

  useEffect(() => {
    setMounted(true);
  }, []);

  useEffect(() => {
    if (!mounted) return;
    if (authLoading) return;

    if (!isAuthenticated || !user || !allowedRoles.includes(user.role)) {
      router.replace('/login');
    }
  }, [mounted, authLoading, isAuthenticated, user, router]);

  if (!mounted || authLoading) {
    return (
      <div className="flex min-h-screen items-center justify-center bg-slate-950 text-white">
        Carregando painel administrativo...
      </div>
    );
  }

  if (!isAuthenticated || !user || !allowedRoles.includes(user.role)) {
    return null;
  }

  return (
    <div className="min-h-screen bg-slate-950 text-white">
      <div className="flex min-h-screen">
        <Sidebar
          collapsed={sidebarCollapsed}
          onToggle={() => setSidebarCollapsed((prev) => !prev)}
        />

        <div
          className={`flex min-h-screen flex-1 flex-col transition-all duration-300 ${
            sidebarCollapsed ? 'md:ml-20' : 'md:ml-72'
          }`}
        >
          <Header
            title="AdministraÃ§Ã£o"
            subtitle="GestÃ£o de moradores, encomendas, usuÃ¡rios e relatÃ³rios"
            onToggleSidebar={() => setSidebarCollapsed((prev) => !prev)}
            sidebarCollapsed={sidebarCollapsed}
          />

          <main className="flex-1 px-4 py-6 md:px-6">{children}</main>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

'use client';

import { useEffect, useMemo, useState } from 'react';
import { useRouter } from 'next/navigation';
import {
  Search,
  RefreshCw,
  Filter,
  Plus,
  Eye,
  Pencil,
  Home,
  UserCheck,
  UserX,
  Clock3,
  MoreHorizontal,
  BadgeCheck,
  CircleOff,
} from 'lucide-react';
import { useAuth } from '@/hooks/use-auth';
import { usePeople } from '@/hooks/use-people';
import { CrudModal } from '@/components/admin/CrudModal';
import MoradorForm, { MoradorFormData } from '@/components/admin/morador-form';
import { api } from '@/lib/axios';
import { Button } from '@/components/ui/button';
import { Card, CardContent, CardHeader, CardTitle } from '@/components/ui/card';
import { Input } from '@/components/ui/input';
import { Badge } from '@/components/ui/badge';
import type { PeopleListResponse, Person, PersonCategory, PersonStatus } from '@/types/person';

type Filters = {
  search: string;
  status: string;
  categoria: string;
};

type MoradorRow = {
  id: string;
  nome: string;
  unidade?: string;
  bloco?: string;
  telefone?: string;
  documento?: string;
  categoria?: string;
  status?: string;
  avatarUrl?: string;
};

function splitUnit(unitId?: string | null) {
  if (!unitId) return { bloco: '', unidade: '' };

  const [bloco = '', ...rest] = unitId.split('-');
  return {
    bloco,
    unidade: rest.join('-'),
  };
}

function mapApiCategoryToUi(category?: string | null, categoryLabel?: string | null) {
  if (categoryLabel) return categoryLabel.toLowerCase();

  switch (category) {
    case 'VISITOR':
      return 'visitante';
    case 'SERVICE_PROVIDER':
      return 'funcionario';
    case 'RENTER':
      return 'locatario';
    case 'RESIDENT':
    default:
      return 'morador';
  }
}

function mapUiCategoryToApi(value: string): PersonCategory {
  switch (value) {
    case 'visitante':
      return 'VISITOR';
    case 'funcionario':
      return 'SERVICE_PROVIDER';
    case 'locatario':
    case 'proprietario':
      return 'RENTER';
    case 'morador':
    default:
      return 'RESIDENT';
  }
}

function safeText(value: unknown, fallback = '') {
  if (value === null || value === undefined) return fallback;
  const text = String(value).trim();
  return text.length ? text : fallback;
}

function mapApiStatusToUi(status?: string | null, statusLabel?: string | null) {
  if (statusLabel) return statusLabel.toLowerCase();

  switch (status) {
    case 'INACTIVE':
      return 'inativo';
    case 'BLOCKED':
      return 'bloqueado';
    case 'ACTIVE':
    default:
      return 'ativo';
  }
}

function mapUiStatusToApi(value: string): PersonStatus {
  switch (value) {
    case 'inativo':
    case 'pendente':
      return 'INACTIVE';
    case 'bloqueado':
      return 'BLOCKED';
    case 'ativo':
    default:
      return 'ACTIVE';
  }
}

function buildUnitId(bloco: string, apartamento: string) {
  const normalizedBloco = bloco.trim();
  const normalizedApartamento = apartamento.trim();

  if (normalizedBloco && normalizedApartamento) {
    return `${normalizedBloco}-${normalizedApartamento}`;
  }

  return normalizedBloco || normalizedApartamento || null;
}

function normalizePeople(data?: PeopleListResponse): MoradorRow[] {
  if (!data?.data) return [];

  return data.data.map((person: Person) => {
    const unit = splitUnit(person.unitId);

    return {
      id: person.id,
      nome: person.name,
      unidade: unit.unidade || person.unitId || '',
      bloco: unit.bloco,
      telefone: person.phone ?? '',
      documento: person.document ?? '',
      categoria: mapApiCategoryToUi(person.category, person.categoryLabel),
      status: mapApiStatusToUi(person.status, person.statusLabel),
      avatarUrl: person.photoUrl ?? '',
    };
  });
}

function normalizeStatus(value: unknown) {
  return safeText(value, 'ativo').toLowerCase();
}

function normalizeCategoria(value: unknown) {
  return safeText(value, 'morador').toLowerCase();
}

function matchesText(row: MoradorRow, term: string) {
  if (!term) return true;
  const query = term.toLowerCase();
  return [
    row.nome,
    row.unidade,
    row.bloco,
    row.telefone,
    row.documento,
    row.categoria,
    row.status,
  ]
    .filter(Boolean)
    .some((value) => String(value).toLowerCase().includes(query));
}

function getErrorMessage(error: unknown, fallback: string) {
  if (typeof error !== 'object' || error === null) return fallback;

  const axiosError = error as {
    response?: {
      data?: {
        detail?: string;
        message?: string;
        error?: string;
      };
    };
    message?: string;
  };

  return (
    axiosError.response?.data?.detail ||
    axiosError.response?.data?.message ||
    axiosError.response?.data?.error ||
    axiosError.message ||
    fallback
  );
}

async function syncPersonStatus(id: string, status: string) {
  await api.patch(`/people/${id}/status`, {
    status: mapUiStatusToApi(status),
  });
}

function StatCard({
  title,
  value,
  icon: Icon,
  hint,
}: {
  title: string;
  value: string;
  icon: React.ComponentType<{ className?: string }>;
  hint: string;
}) {
  return (
    <Card className="border-white/10 bg-white/5 text-white">
      <CardHeader className="flex flex-row items-start justify-between space-y-0 pb-2">
        <CardTitle className="text-sm font-medium text-slate-300">{title}</CardTitle>
        <Icon className="h-4 w-4 text-slate-400" />
      </CardHeader>
      <CardContent>
        <div className="text-2xl font-semibold">{value}</div>
        <p className="mt-1 text-xs text-slate-400">{hint}</p>
      </CardContent>
    </Card>
  );
}

export default function MoradoresPage() {
  const router = useRouter();
  const { user, loading: authLoading, isAuthenticated } = useAuth();
  const {
    data: peopleData,
    isLoading: peopleLoading,
    error: peopleError,
    refetch: refetchPeople,
  } = usePeople({ limit: 100 });

  const [mounted, setMounted] = useState(false);
  const [filters, setFilters] = useState<Filters>({
    search: '',
    status: 'all',
    categoria: 'all',
  });
  const [openCreate, setOpenCreate] = useState(false);
  const [openEdit, setOpenEdit] = useState(false);
  const [selectedMorador, setSelectedMorador] = useState<MoradorRow | null>(null);
  const [saving, setSaving] = useState(false);
  const [deletingId, setDeletingId] = useState<string | null>(null);

  useEffect(() => {
    setMounted(true);
  }, []);

  useEffect(() => {
    if (!mounted || authLoading) return;

    if (!isAuthenticated || !user) {
      router.replace('/login');
      return;
    }

    if (!['ADMIN', 'MASTER'].includes(String(user.role))) {
      router.replace('/admin');
    }
  }, [mounted, authLoading, isAuthenticated, user, router]);

  const moradores = useMemo(() => normalizePeople(peopleData), [peopleData]);

  const filteredMoradores = useMemo(() => {
    return moradores.filter((row) => {
      const status = normalizeStatus(row.status);
      const categoria = normalizeCategoria(row.categoria);

      const statusOk = filters.status === 'all' || status === filters.status;
      const categoriaOk = filters.categoria === 'all' || categoria === filters.categoria;
      const searchOk = matchesText(row, filters.search);

      return statusOk && categoriaOk && searchOk;
    });
  }, [moradores, filters]);

  const stats = useMemo(() => {
    const total = moradores.length;
    const ativos = moradores.filter((item) => normalizeStatus(item.status) === 'ativo').length;
    const pendentes = moradores.filter((item) => normalizeStatus(item.status) === 'pendente').length;
    const bloqueados = moradores.filter((item) => normalizeStatus(item.status) === 'bloqueado').length;

    return { total, ativos, pendentes, bloqueados };
  }, [moradores]);

  const handleRefresh = async () => {
    await refetchPeople();
  };

  const openNewMorador = () => {
    setSelectedMorador(null);
    setOpenCreate(true);
  };

  const openEditMorador = (morador: MoradorRow) => {
    setSelectedMorador(morador);
    setOpenEdit(true);
  };

  const closeModals = () => {
    setOpenCreate(false);
    setOpenEdit(false);
    setSelectedMorador(null);
  };

  async function createMorador(data: MoradorFormData) {
    setSaving(true);
    try {
      const response = await api.post<Person>('/people', {
        name: data.nome,
        phone: data.telefone,
        document: data.documento,
        category: mapUiCategoryToApi(data.tipo),
        unitId: buildUnitId(data.bloco, data.apartamento),
      });

      if (data.status !== 'ativo') {
        await syncPersonStatus(response.data.id, data.status);
      }

      setOpenCreate(false);
      await handleRefresh();
    } catch (error) {
      throw new Error(getErrorMessage(error, 'Erro ao criar morador'));
    } finally {
      setSaving(false);
    }
  }

  async function updateMorador(data: MoradorFormData) {
    if (!selectedMorador?.id) return;

    setSaving(true);
    try {
      await api.put(`/people/${selectedMorador.id}`, {
        name: data.nome,
        phone: data.telefone,
        document: data.documento,
        category: mapUiCategoryToApi(data.tipo),
        unitId: buildUnitId(data.bloco, data.apartamento),
      });

      await syncPersonStatus(selectedMorador.id, data.status);

      setOpenEdit(false);
      setSelectedMorador(null);
      await handleRefresh();
    } catch (error) {
      throw new Error(getErrorMessage(error, 'Erro ao atualizar morador'));
    } finally {
      setSaving(false);
    }
  }

  async function deleteMorador(id: string) {
    const confirmed = window.confirm('Deseja excluir este morador?');
    if (!confirmed) return;

    setDeletingId(id);
    try {
      await api.delete(`/people/${id}`);
      await handleRefresh();
    } catch (error) {
      throw new Error(getErrorMessage(error, 'Erro ao excluir morador'));
    } finally {
      setDeletingId(null);
    }
  }

  if (!mounted || authLoading) {
    return (
      <div className="flex min-h-[60vh] items-center justify-center rounded-3xl border border-white/10 bg-white/5 text-white">
        Carregando painel...
      </div>
    );
  }

  if (!isAuthenticated || !user) {
    return null;
  }

  return (
    <div className="space-y-6 text-white">
      <section className="rounded-3xl border border-white/10 bg-white/5 p-5 backdrop-blur">
        <div className="flex flex-col gap-4 lg:flex-row lg:items-end lg:justify-between">
          <div>
            <p className="text-xs uppercase tracking-[0.22em] text-slate-400">AdministraÃ§Ã£o</p>
            <h1 className="mt-2 text-2xl font-semibold">Moradores</h1>
            <p className="mt-2 max-w-2xl text-sm text-slate-400">
              Cadastro, ediÃ§Ã£o e gerenciamento de moradores com integraÃ§Ã£o direta Ã  API real.
            </p>
          </div>

          <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-3">
            <Button
              onClick={openNewMorador}
              className="inline-flex items-center gap-2 rounded-xl bg-white px-4 py-3 text-slate-950 hover:bg-slate-200"
            >
              <Plus className="h-4 w-4" />
              Novo
            </Button>

            <Button
              variant="outline"
              onClick={handleRefresh}
              className="inline-flex items-center gap-2 border-white/10 bg-white/5 text-white hover:bg-white/10"
            >
              <RefreshCw className="h-4 w-4" />
              Atualizar
            </Button>
          </div>
        </div>
      </section>

      <section className="grid gap-4 md:grid-cols-2 xl:grid-cols-4">
        <StatCard
          title="Total de moradores"
          value={peopleLoading ? '...' : String(stats.total)}
          icon={Home}
          hint="Registros carregados da API"
        />
        <StatCard
          title="Ativos"
          value={peopleLoading ? '...' : String(stats.ativos)}
          icon={UserCheck}
          hint="Moradores liberados"
        />
        <StatCard
          title="Pendentes"
          value={peopleLoading ? '...' : String(stats.pendentes)}
          icon={Clock3}
          hint="Aguardando validaÃ§Ã£o"
        />
        <StatCard
          title="Bloqueados"
          value={peopleLoading ? '...' : String(stats.bloqueados)}
          icon={UserX}
          hint="Acesso restrito"
        />
      </section>

      <section className="rounded-3xl border border-white/10 bg-white/5 p-5 backdrop-blur">
        <div className="grid gap-3 lg:grid-cols-[1.5fr_0.8fr_0.8fr]">
          <label className="flex items-center gap-3 rounded-2xl border border-white/10 bg-slate-950/60 px-4 py-3">
            <Search className="h-4 w-4 text-slate-400" />
            <Input
              value={filters.search}
              onChange={(e) => setFilters((prev) => ({ ...prev, search: e.target.value }))}
              placeholder="Buscar por nome, bloco, telefone, documento..."
              className="border-0 bg-transparent p-0 text-white shadow-none placeholder:text-slate-500 focus-visible:ring-0"
            />
          </label>

          <label className="rounded-2xl border border-white/10 bg-slate-950/60 px-4 py-3">
            <select
              value={filters.status}
              onChange={(e) => setFilters((prev) => ({ ...prev, status: e.target.value }))}
              className="w-full bg-transparent text-sm outline-none"
            >
              <option value="all">Todos os status</option>
              <option value="ativo">Ativo</option>
              <option value="pendente">Pendente</option>
              <option value="inativo">Inativo</option>
              <option value="bloqueado">Bloqueado</option>
            </select>
          </label>

          <label className="rounded-2xl border border-white/10 bg-slate-950/60 px-4 py-3">
            <select
              value={filters.categoria}
              onChange={(e) => setFilters((prev) => ({ ...prev, categoria: e.target.value }))}
              className="w-full bg-transparent text-sm outline-none"
            >
              <option value="all">Todas as categorias</option>
              <option value="morador">Morador</option>
              <option value="proprietario">ProprietÃ¡rio</option>
              <option value="locatario">LocatÃ¡rio</option>
              <option value="funcionario">FuncionÃ¡rio</option>
              <option value="visitante">Visitante</option>
            </select>
          </label>
        </div>
      </section>

      {peopleError ? (
        <div className="rounded-3xl border border-red-500/30 bg-red-500/10 p-5 text-sm text-red-100">
          NÃ£o foi possÃ­vel carregar os moradores.
        </div>
      ) : null}

      <section className="overflow-hidden rounded-3xl border border-white/10 bg-white/5 backdrop-blur">
        <div className="flex items-center justify-between border-b border-white/10 px-5 py-4">
          <div>
            <h2 className="text-lg font-semibold">Lista de moradores</h2>
            <p className="text-sm text-slate-400">
              {filteredMoradores.length} registro(s) encontrado(s)
            </p>
          </div>
          <Filter className="h-5 w-5 text-slate-400" />
        </div>

        {filteredMoradores.length === 0 ? (
          <div className="px-5 py-10">
            <div className="rounded-2xl border border-dashed border-white/10 bg-slate-950/50 p-8 text-center">
              <CircleOff className="mx-auto h-10 w-10 text-slate-400" />
              <h3 className="mt-3 text-base font-medium">Nenhum morador encontrado</h3>
              <p className="mt-1 text-sm text-slate-400">
                Ajuste os filtros ou clique em Novo para cadastrar.
              </p>
            </div>
          </div>
        ) : (
          <div className="divide-y divide-white/10">
            {filteredMoradores.map((morador) => (
              <div
                key={morador.id}
                className="grid gap-4 px-5 py-4 lg:grid-cols-[1.2fr_0.7fr_0.7fr_0.6fr_auto] lg:items-center"
              >
                <div>
                  <p className="font-medium text-white">{morador.nome}</p>
                  <p className="text-sm text-slate-400">
                    {safeText(morador.bloco, 'â€”')} / {safeText(morador.unidade, 'â€”')}
                  </p>
                </div>

                <div className="text-sm text-slate-300">
                  {safeText(morador.telefone, 'Sem telefone')}
                </div>

                <div className="text-sm text-slate-300">
                  {safeText(morador.documento, 'Sem documento')}
                </div>

                <div>
                  <Badge
                    className={
                      normalizeStatus(morador.status) === 'ativo'
                        ? 'bg-emerald-500/15 text-emerald-300 hover:bg-emerald-500/20'
                        : normalizeStatus(morador.status) === 'pendente'
                          ? 'bg-amber-500/15 text-amber-300 hover:bg-amber-500/20'
                          : normalizeStatus(morador.status) === 'bloqueado'
                            ? 'bg-red-500/15 text-red-300 hover:bg-red-500/20'
                            : 'bg-slate-500/15 text-slate-300 hover:bg-slate-500/20'
                    }
                  >
                    {safeText(morador.status, 'ativo')}
                  </Badge>
                </div>

                <div className="flex items-center justify-end gap-2">
                  <Button
                    size="icon"
                    variant="outline"
                    className="border-white/10 bg-white/5 text-white hover:bg-white/10"
                    aria-label="Visualizar morador"
                  >
                    <Eye className="h-4 w-4" />
                  </Button>

                  <Button
                    size="icon"
                    variant="outline"
                    onClick={() => openEditMorador(morador)}
                    className="border-white/10 bg-white/5 text-white hover:bg-white/10"
                    aria-label="Editar morador"
                  >
                    <Pencil className="h-4 w-4" />
                  </Button>

                  <Button
                    size="icon"
                    variant="outline"
                    onClick={() => deleteMorador(morador.id)}
                    disabled={deletingId === morador.id}
                    className="border-white/10 bg-white/5 text-white hover:bg-white/10"
                    aria-label="Excluir morador"
                  >
                    <MoreHorizontal className="h-4 w-4" />
                  </Button>
                </div>
              </div>
            ))}
          </div>
        )}
      </section>

      <CrudModal
        open={openCreate}
        title="Novo morador"
        description="Cadastre um novo morador na API externa."
        onClose={closeModals}
        maxWidth="xl"
      >
        <MoradorForm
          onSubmit={createMorador}
          onCancel={closeModals}
          loading={saving}
        />
      </CrudModal>

      <CrudModal
        open={openEdit}
        title="Editar morador"
        description="Atualize os dados do morador selecionado."
        onClose={closeModals}
        maxWidth="xl"
      >
        <MoradorForm
          initialData={
            selectedMorador
              ? {
                  nome: selectedMorador.nome,
                  email: '',
                  telefone: selectedMorador.telefone ?? '',
                  documento: selectedMorador.documento ?? '',
                  bloco: selectedMorador.bloco ?? '',
                  apartamento: selectedMorador.unidade ?? '',
                  tipo: normalizeCategoria(selectedMorador.categoria),
                  status: normalizeStatus(selectedMorador.status),
                }
              : undefined
          }
          onSubmit={updateMorador}
          onCancel={closeModals}
          loading={saving}
        />
      </CrudModal>
    </div>
  );
}

ARQUIVO: src\app\admin\page.tsx

'use client';

import { useEffect, useMemo, useState } from 'react';
import { useRouter } from 'next/navigation';
import { useAuth } from '@/hooks/use-auth';
import { usePeople } from '@/hooks/use-people';
import { useAlerts } from '@/hooks/use-alerts';
import { useCameras } from '@/hooks/use-cameras';

type StatCardProps = {
  label: string;
  value: string;
  helper: string;
};

function StatCard({ label, value, helper }: StatCardProps) {
  return (
    <div className="rounded-2xl border border-white/10 bg-white/5 p-4 backdrop-blur">
      <p className="text-sm text-slate-300">{label}</p>
      <p className="mt-2 text-3xl font-semibold text-white">{value}</p>
      <p className="mt-2 text-xs text-slate-400">{helper}</p>
    </div>
  );
}

type EmptyStateProps = {
  title: string;
  description: string;
};

function EmptyState({ title, description }: EmptyStateProps) {
  return (
    <div className="rounded-2xl border border-dashed border-white/10 bg-white/5 p-6 text-center">
      <h3 className="text-base font-medium text-white">{title}</h3>
      <p className="mt-2 text-sm text-slate-400">{description}</p>
    </div>
  );
}

export default function AdminPage() {
  const router = useRouter();
  const { user, loading: authLoading, isAuthenticated } = useAuth();

  const allowedRoles = useMemo(
    () => ['ADMIN', 'MASTER'],
    []
  );

  const [mounted, setMounted] = useState(false);

  const {
    data: peopleData,
    isLoading: peopleLoading,
    error: peopleError,
  } = usePeople({ limit: 20 });

  const {
    data: alertsData,
    isLoading: alertsLoading,
    error: alertsError,
  } = useAlerts({ limit: 20 });

  const {
    data: camerasData,
    isLoading: camerasLoading,
    error: camerasError,
  } = useCameras();

  useEffect(() => {
    setMounted(true);
  }, []);

  useEffect(() => {
    if (!mounted) return;

    if (authLoading) return;

    if (!isAuthenticated || !user || !allowedRoles.includes(user.role)) {
      router.replace('/login');
      return;
    }
  }, [mounted, authLoading, isAuthenticated, user, router, allowedRoles]);

  const people = Array.isArray((peopleData as any)?.data)
    ? (peopleData as any).data
    : Array.isArray(peopleData)
      ? peopleData
      : [];

  const alerts = Array.isArray((alertsData as any)?.data)
    ? (alertsData as any).data
    : Array.isArray(alertsData)
      ? alertsData
      : [];

  const cameras = Array.isArray((camerasData as any)?.data)
    ? (camerasData as any).data
    : Array.isArray(camerasData)
      ? camerasData
      : [];

  const activePeople = people.filter((item: any) => {
    const status = String(item.status || item.estado || '').toLowerCase();
    return status === 'ativo' || status === 'active' || status === 'ativo';
  });

  const openAlerts = alerts.filter((item: any) => {
    const status = String(item.status || '').toLowerCase();
    return status === 'aberto' || status === 'open' || status === 'pendente';
  });

  const onlineCameras = cameras.filter((item: any) => {
    const status = String(item.status || '').toLowerCase();
    return status === 'online' || status === 'ativo' || status === 'active';
  });

  if (!mounted || authLoading) {
    return (
      <div className="flex min-h-screen items-center justify-center bg-slate-950 text-white">
        Carregando dashboard...
      </div>
    );
  }

  if (!isAuthenticated || !user || !allowedRoles.includes(user.role)) {
    return null;
  }

  return (
    <div className="min-h-screen bg-[#07111f] text-white">
      <div className="mx-auto max-w-[1600px] space-y-6 p-4 md:p-6">
        <header className="rounded-3xl border border-white/10 bg-white/5 p-5 shadow-xl backdrop-blur">
          <div className="flex flex-col gap-4 md:flex-row md:items-end md:justify-between">
            <div>
              <p className="text-xs uppercase tracking-[0.2em] text-slate-400">
                Painel administrativo
              </p>
              <h1 className="mt-2 text-3xl font-semibold text-white">
                Dashboard do Admin
              </h1>
              <p className="mt-2 max-w-3xl text-sm text-slate-300">
                VisÃ£o consolidada para gestÃ£o de moradores, alertas, cÃ¢meras e operaÃ§Ã£o,
                com base na API real e pronta para evoluÃ§Ã£o por perfil de usuÃ¡rio.
              </p>
            </div>

            <div className="rounded-2xl border border-white/10 bg-black/20 px-4 py-3">
              <p className="text-xs text-slate-400">SessÃ£o ativa</p>
              <p className="mt-1 text-sm font-medium text-white">
                {user.name}
              </p>
              <p className="text-xs text-slate-400">{user.email}</p>
            </div>
          </div>
        </header>

        <section className="grid gap-4 md:grid-cols-2 xl:grid-cols-4">
          <StatCard
            label="Moradores / Pessoas"
            value={peopleLoading ? '...' : String(people.length)}
            helper="Total carregado da API"
          />
          <StatCard
            label="Ativos"
            value={peopleLoading ? '...' : String(activePeople.length)}
            helper="Com status ativo"
          />
          <StatCard
            label="Alertas abertos"
            value={alertsLoading ? '...' : String(openAlerts.length)}
            helper="PendÃªncias de monitoramento"
          />
          <StatCard
            label="CÃ¢meras online"
            value={camerasLoading ? '...' : String(onlineCameras.length)}
            helper="DisponÃ­veis para operaÃ§Ã£o"
          />
        </section>

        <div className="grid gap-6 xl:grid-cols-[1.3fr_0.9fr]">

            <section className="rounded-3xl border border-white/10 bg-white/5 p-5 backdrop-blur">

                  <h2 className="text-lg font-semibold text-white">
                    Resumo operacional
                  </h2>

                    Indicadores principais para decisÃ£o rÃ¡pida.

                <div className="rounded-2xl border border-white/10 bg-slate-950/60 p-4">
                  <p className="text-xs uppercase tracking-[0.18em] text-slate-500">
                    Base

                />

                />

                <div className="overflow-hidden rounded-2xl border border-white/10">
                  <div className="grid grid-cols-12 bg-white/5 px-4 py-3 text-xs uppercase tracking-[0.16em] text-slate-400">

                  </div>

                        key={person.id}
                        className="grid grid-cols-12 items-center px-4 py-4 text-sm"
                      >
                        <div className="col-span-4 font-medium text-white">
                          {person.name || person.nome || 'Sem nome'}
                        </div>

                          {person.category || person.categoria || '-'}

                            {person.status || 'ATIVO'}
                          </span>
                        </div>
                        <div className="col-span-2 truncate text-xs text-slate-400">

          </main>

          <aside className="space-y-6">

              <div className="mb-4">
                <h2 className="text-lg font-semibold text-white">Alertas recentes</h2>
                <p className="text-sm text-slate-400">
                  OcorrÃªncias e pendÃªncias mais recentes.
                </p>
              </div>

              {alertsError ? (
                <EmptyState
                  title="NÃ£o foi possÃ­vel carregar alertas"
                  description="Verifique o endpoint de alertas."
                />
              ) : alerts.length === 0 ? (
                <EmptyState
                  title="Sem alertas"
                  description="A lista aparecerÃ¡ aqui quando houver eventos."
                />
              ) : (
                <div className="space-y-3">
                  {alerts.slice(0, 6).map((alert: any) => (
                    <div
                      key={alert.id}
                      className="rounded-2xl border border-white/10 bg-slate-950/60 p-4"
                    >
                      <div className="flex items-center justify-between gap-3">
                        <h3 className="text-sm font-medium text-white">
                          {alert.title || alert.message || 'Alerta'}
                        </h3>
                        <span className="rounded-full bg-yellow-400/10 px-2.5 py-1 text-[11px] font-medium text-yellow-300">
                          {alert.status || 'PENDENTE'}
                        </span>
                      </div>
                      <p className="mt-2 text-sm text-slate-400">
                        {alert.description || 'Sem descriÃ§Ã£o disponÃ­vel.'}
                      </p>
                    </div>
                  ))}
                </div>
              )}
            </section>

            <section className="rounded-3xl border border-white/10 bg-white/5 p-5 backdrop-blur">
              <div className="mb-4">
                <h2 className="text-lg font-semibold text-white">CÃ¢meras online</h2>
                <p className="text-sm text-slate-400">
                  Estado atual do parque de cÃ¢meras.
                </p>
              </div>

              {camerasError ? (
                <EmptyState
                  title="NÃ£o foi possÃ­vel carregar cÃ¢meras"
                  description="Confira o endpoint e a resposta da API."
                />
              ) : cameras.length === 0 ? (
                <EmptyState
                  title="Sem cÃ¢meras"
                  description="Os dispositivos aparecerÃ£o aqui quando a API responder."
                />
              ) : (
                <div className="grid gap-3">
                  {cameras.slice(0, 6).map((camera: any) => (
                    <div
                      key={camera.id}
                      className="rounded-2xl border border-white/10 bg-slate-950/60 p-4"
                    >
                      <div className="flex items-center justify-between gap-3">
                        <h3 className="text-sm font-medium text-white">
                          {camera.name || camera.nome || 'CÃ¢mera'}
                        </h3>
                        <span className="rounded-full bg-emerald-400/10 px-2.5 py-1 text-[11px] font-medium text-emerald-300">
                          {camera.status || 'ONLINE'}
                        </span>
                      </div>
                      <p className="mt-2 text-sm text-slate-400">
                        {camera.location || camera.localizacao || 'Local nÃ£o informado'}
                      </p>
                    </div>
                  ))}
                </div>
              )}
            </section>
          </aside>
        </div>

        <footer className="pb-2 text-center text-xs text-slate-500">
          Dashboard preparado para evoluÃ§Ã£o por perfis: MASTER, ADMIN, OPERADOR e CENTRAL.
        </footer>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}
